Candrakiraṇa Manuscript Perpusnas L298: Digital Diplomatic Edition

Author of digital edition: Zakariya Pamuji Aminullah

Filename: DHARMA_DiplEdCandrakiranaPerpusnasL298.xml

Language: Old Javanese

Repository: Nusantara Philology (tfd-nusantara-philology)

Version: part commented since without access_token with github actions api calls are limited – still working on it

Witness

  • Jakarta, Perpustakaan Nasional Republik Indonesia, Koleksi Naskah Nusantara, L. 298
    • Physical Description: Palm-leaf manuscript. 47 leaves in ‘Merapi-Merbabu’ script, using layar in Indonesian mode. Apparently written in year 1564 of an uncertain era.
    • History: In ... 18.., ... found this manuscript at ....

Edition

(1)(2)(3)

Apparatus


^1. ,,,,,,,] • These marks are written by scribe with assumption that the condition of manuscript source was already corrupt during copying process.
^2. Apa] • The scribe seems wrote {R̥} at first, then the bottom part of the akṣara is crossed out so that akṣara would be read as pa.
^3. ⟦,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,⟧] • According to the photo of folio 26, it is evident that the commas is actually the signs from the scribe for tagging the palm leaf part which was already torn while he was using it.

These marks are written by scribe with assumption that the condition of manuscript source was already corrupt during copying process.Apa
The scribe seems wrote {R̥} at first, then the bottom part of the akṣara is crossed out so that akṣara would be read as pa. ⟦,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,⟧
According to the photo of folio 26, it is evident that the commas is actually the signs from the scribe for tagging the palm leaf part which was already torn while he was using it.
